             /* Set the width of the side navigation to 250px and the left margin of the page content to 250px */
 function openNav() {
     document.getElementById("mySidenav").style.width = "250px";
 //     document.getElementById("main").style.marginLeft = "250px";
   $("#hamburger-icon").addClass("active");
 }
 
 /* Set the width of the side navigation to 0 and the left margin of the page content to 0 */
 function closeNav() {
     document.getElementById("mySidenav").style.width = "0";
 //     document.getElementById("main").style.marginLeft = "0";
   $("#hamburger-icon").removeClass("active");
 }
   
   $(document).ready(function(){
     
     $(document).on("click", ".burger-tier-one", function(){
       var tierTwo = $(this).next(".burger-tier-two"),
           tierTwoHidden = tierTwo.hasClass("hidden");
       $(".burger-tier-two").addClass("hidden");
       if (tierTwoHidden) {
         tierTwo.removeClass("hidden");
       }
     });
     
     $(document).on("click", "#hamburger-icon", function(){
       if ( $(this).hasClass("active") ) {
         closeNav();
       } else {
         openNav();
       }
     });
     
         $(window).resize(function(){
             var $navHeight = $(window).height() - $('.navbar-container-inner').height();
             $('.sidenav').css({'max-height': $navHeight});
         });
     
   });
            </script>

             </span>
            </button>
            <h4 class="modal-title" id="nextDayModalLabel">
             Next day delivery
            </h4>
           </div>
           <div class="modal-body">
            <p>
             For your information we display the amount of stock we are holding on the product page
            </p>
            <p style="color: #A3C54C">
             If you see either a number of items in stock, or simply In Stock this means that we have these items on hand in our warehouse and they can be shipped out the same day if you order before 2.00pm*
            </p>
            <p>
             Where your basket consists of all stocked items we display the option to select a next day delivery service. If you have ordered your item before the daily cut off time your order will be delivered next working day!*
            </p>
            <p>
             * 24 hour carrier service does not deliver on Saturday, Sunday or bank holidays. Place your order by 2.00pm for the order to be dispatched same day.
            </p>

                 "productjson": 3,
                 "basketjson": 4
     };
   
   var carouselOptions = {
     "homejson": {
       "items": 4,
       "itemsMobile": [576, 2],
       "itemsTablet": [767, 3],
       "itemsDesktopSmall": [991, 4],
       "itemsDesktop": [1199, 4]
     },
     "homejson2": {
       "items": 7,
       "itemsMobile": [576, 2],
       "itemsTablet": [767, 3],
       "itemsDesktopSmall": [991, 5],
       "itemsDesktop": [1199, 7]
     },
     "categoryjson2": {
       "items": 3,
       "itemsMobile": [576, 2],
       "itemsTablet": [767, 2],
       "itemsDesktopSmall": [991, 3],
       "itemsDesktop": [1199, 3]
     },
     "categoryjson": {
       "items": 4,
       "itemsMobile": [576, 2],
       "itemsTablet": [767, 3],
       "itemsDesktopSmall": [991, 4],
       "itemsDesktop": [1199, 4]
     },
     "productjson": {
       "items": 3,
       "itemsMobile": [576, 2],
       "itemsTablet": [767, 3],
       "itemsDesktopSmall": [991, 3],
       "itemsDesktop": [1199, 3]
     },
     "basketjson": {
       "items": 4,
       "itemsMobile": [576, 2],
       "itemsTablet": [767, 3],
       "itemsDesktopSmall": [991, 4],
       "itemsDesktop": [1199, 4]
     }
   };
 
   
   	var PeeriusCallbacks={
       track: track,
 			
       smartRecs:function(jsonData) {
 // console.log("peerius", jsonData);
             jsonData.forEach(function(data){
              if (data.position == 'homejson2' || data.position == 'homejson' || data.position == 'categoryjson2' || data.position == 'categoryjson' || data.position == 'product json' || data.position == 'basketjson') {
                 dataPosition = data.position.replace(/\s+/g, '');
                if (positions.indexOf(dataPosition) == -1) {
                  positions.push(dataPosition);
                }
                 data.recs.forEach(function(rec){
                   
 
 					var rec_img200x = rec.img.replace(/\.([^\.]*)$/, "_200x."+"$1");
                   
                     var rec_url = rec.url.replace(/\?variant=[\d]+$/, "");
                   
                     var rating = parseInt(rec.attributes.rating),
                         ratingStr = '';
                   
                     var discount = 100 - Math.ceil(rec.prices.GBP.salePrice / rec.prices.GBP.unitPrice * 100),
                         discountStr = '';
                   
                     var featuredStr = '';
                   if (data.position == 'categoryjson2') {
                     featuredStr = '<span class="featured-thumb" style="background:  none repeat scroll 0 0;">featured</span>';
                   }
                   
                   if (discount > 0) {
                     discountStr = '<div class="p-rollover-background"></div><div class="market-price" style="background: "> <div class="price-save"><span class="label" style="color: ">save</span><span class="procent"> ' + discount + '<span class="p">%</span></span><span class="now" style="color: ">now</span></div> </div>';
                   }
 
                     if (rating > 0) {
                         ratingStr += '<span>';
                         for (var r=0; r<rating; r++) {
                             ratingStr += '<i class="fa fa-star" aria-hidden="true"></i>';
                         }
                         if (rating < 5) {
                             for (var r=0; r<5-rating; r++) {
                                 ratingStr += '<i class="fa fa-star-o" aria-hidden="true"></i>';
                             }
                         }
                         ratingStr += '</span>';
                         ratingStr += '<span class="pull-right rating-number">' + rec.attributes.reviews + ' Reviews</span>';
                     }
 
                     var item = [
                         '<div class="col-md-12 item-peerius">',
                           '<a href="' + rec_url + '" onclick="Peerius.smartRecsClick('+rec.id+');">',
                             '<div class="item-rating">',
                                 ratingStr,
                             '</div>',
                             '<div class="item-image">',
                                 '<img src="' + rec_img200x + '" />',
                       			discountStr,
                       			featuredStr,
                             '</div>',
                             '<div class="item-label" style="background: #CC0504 none repeat scroll 0 0;">',
                                 '<div>VIEW NOW<i class="fa fa-chevron-circle-right"></i></div>',
                             '</div>',
                             '<div class="item-name-price text-center">',
                       			'<div class="item-name"><span>' + rec.title + '</span></div>',
                                 '<div class="item-price"><strong>from &pound;' + rec.prices.GBP.salePrice.toFixed(2) + '</strong></div>',
                             '</div>',
                           '</a>',
                         '</div>'
                     ].join('');
                     $('.js-pd-peerius-' + dataPosition).append(item);
                   
                   var image = new Image();
                   image.src = rec_img200x;
                   image.onload = function() {
                     // image exists and is loaded, so nothing to do here
                   }
                   image.onerror = function() {
                     // image did not load, replace src to original
                     $('img[src="' + rec_img200x + '"]').attr('src', rec.img);
                   }
 
                 })
             }
               
         });
 
 
         $(document).ready(function() {
 
           for (pos in positions) {
             $('.js-pd-peerius-' + positions[pos]).owlCarousel({
               nav:true,
               items: carouselOptions[ positions[pos] ].items,
               itemsMobile: carouselOptions[ positions[pos] ].itemsMobile,
               itemsTablet: carouselOptions[ positions[pos] ].itemsTablet,
               itemsDesktopSmall: carouselOptions[ positions[pos] ].itemsDesktopSmall,
               itemsDesktop: carouselOptions[ positions[pos] ].itemsDesktop,
             });
           }
 
           $(".peerius-inner").removeClass("hide");
 
         });
 
       }
     }
       </script>
